LooseVersion is provided by Python distutils, which is going away in
3.12. This PR vendors _pep440 from scipy and uses it as a replacement.
Numpy distutils is not touched, replacing LooseVersion in that package
was considered too risky, and numpy distutils will need to go away when
Python distutils does." class="Link--secondary" href="/numpy/numpy/commit/df8d1fd3c2077ca785b0948912162e03727ace6c">MAINT: Replace LooseVersion by _pep440.</a>

            <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a><a href="https://numpy.org/" rel="nofollow"><img alt="NumPy" src="/numpy/numpy/raw/main/branding/logo/primary/numpylogo.svg" height="60" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></h1>










<p dir="auto"><a href="https://numfocus.org" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/42ca0da5f59b4fa9dd410434fa62cf8942c437d06669273fa7783c15d1be9cee/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f706f776572656425323062792d4e756d464f4355532d6f72616e67652e7376673f7374796c653d666c617426636f6c6f72413d45313532334426636f6c6f72423d303037443841" alt="Powered by NumFOCUS" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/powered%20by-NumFOCUS-orange.svg?style=flat&amp;colorA=E1523D&amp;colorB=007D8A" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://pypi.org/project/numpy/" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/f8b8ac0ab4f6ba80c171ccbc686e7764bf1f21dfdbcfc737d0278f386fd34122/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f707970692f646d2f6e756d70792e7376673f6c6162656c3d50795049253230646f776e6c6f616473" alt="PyPI Downloads" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/pypi/dm/numpy.svg?label=PyPI%20downloads" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://anaconda.org/conda-forge/numpy" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c0a6a49d7ce26df2e4d840a1dd5040297d43a512e7d487bc2e2797422a774aed/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f636f6e64612f646e2f636f6e64612d666f7267652f6e756d70792e7376673f6c6162656c3d436f6e6461253230646f776e6c6f616473" alt="Conda Downloads" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/conda/dn/conda-forge/numpy.svg?label=Conda%20downloads" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/tagged/numpy" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/627b1e50b958cb52a27d1da3a8bba2eebba670ca60f2f1092079268f54d7449f/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f737461636b6f766572666c6f772d41736b2532307175657374696f6e732d626c75652e737667" alt="Stack Overflow" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/stackoverflow-Ask%20questions-blue.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="https://doi.org/10.1038/s41586-020-2649-2" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/9b2d3d12826d6b027d9853646f7c60e287589f356da17a134c997853e96fa9c1/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f444f492d31302e313033382532467334313539322d2d3031392d2d303638362d2d322d626c7565" alt="Nature Paper" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/DOI-10.1038%2Fs41592--019--0686--2-blue" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">NumPy is the fundamental package for scientific computing with Python.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>Website:</strong> <a href="https://www.numpy.org" rel="nofollow">https://www.numpy.org</a></li>
<li><strong>Documentation:</strong> <a href="https://numpy.org/doc" rel="nofollow">https://numpy.org/doc</a></li>
<li><strong>Mailing list:</strong> <a href="https://mail.python.org/mailman/listinfo/numpy-discussion" rel="nofollow">https://mail.python.org/mailman/listinfo/numpy-discussion</a></li>
<li><strong>Source code:</strong> <a href="https://github.com/numpy/numpy">https://github.com/numpy/numpy</a></li>
<li><strong>Contributing:</strong> <a href="https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/dev/index.html" rel="nofollow">https://www.numpy.org/devdocs/dev/index.html</a></li>
<li><strong>Bug reports:</strong> <a href="https://github.com/numpy/numpy/issues">https://github.com/numpy/numpy/issues</a></li>
<li><strong>Report a security vulnerability:</strong> <a href="https://tidelift.com/docs/security" rel="nofollow">https://tidelift.com/docs/security</a></li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">It provides:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>a powerful N-dimensional array object</li>
<li>sophisticated (broadcasting) functions</li>
<li>tools for integrating C/C++ and Fortran code</li>
<li>useful linear algebra, Fourier transform, and random number capabilities</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Testing:</p>
<p dir="auto">NumPy requires <code>pytest</code> and <code>hypothesis</code>.  Tests can then be run after installation with:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto"><pre><code>python -c 'import numpy; numpy.test()'
</code></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container position-absolute right-0 top-0">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy" class="ClipboardButton btn js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 tooltipped-no-delay" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="python -c 'import numpy; numpy.test()'" tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon m-2">
    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 010 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 00-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 00.25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 011.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 019.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 010 14.25v-7.5z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0114.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 015 9.25v-7.5zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 00-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 00.25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 00-.25-.25h-7.5z"></path>

    <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 010 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 01-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.75.75 0 011.06-1.06L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 011.06 0z"></path>

<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-code-of-conduct" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#code-of-conduct"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Code of Conduct</h2>
<p dir="auto">NumPy is a community-driven open source project developed by a diverse group of
<a href="https://numpy.org/teams/" rel="nofollow">contributors</a>. The NumPy leadership has made a strong
commitment to creating an open, inclusive, and positive community. Please read the
<a href="https://numpy.org/code-of-conduct/" rel="nofollow">NumPy Code of Conduct</a> for guidance on how to interact
with others in a way that makes our community thrive.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-call-for-contributions" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#call-for-contributions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Call for Contributions</h2>
<p dir="auto">The NumPy project welcomes your expertise and enthusiasm!</p>
<p dir="auto">Small improvements or fixes are always appreciated; issues labeled as <a href="https://github.com/numpy/numpy/labels/good%20first%20issue">"good
first issue"</a>
may be a good starting point. If you are considering larger contributions
to the source code, please contact us through the <a href="https://mail.python.org/mailman/listinfo/numpy-discussion" rel="nofollow">mailing
list</a> first.</p>
<p dir="auto">Writing code isn’t the only way to contribute to NumPy. You can also:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>review pull requests</li>
<li>help us stay on top of new and old issues</li>
<li>develop tutorials, presentations, and other educational materials</li>
<li>maintain and improve <a href="https://github.com/numpy/numpy.org">our website</a></li>
<li>develop graphic design for our brand assets and promotional materials</li>
<li>translate website content</li>
<li>help with outreach and onboard new contributors</li>
<li>write grant proposals and help with other fundraising efforts</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">For more information about the ways you can contribute to NumPy, visit <a href="https://numpy.org/contribute/" rel="nofollow">our website</a>.
If you’re unsure where to start or how your skills fit in, reach out! You can
ask on the mailing list or here, on GitHub, by opening a new issue or leaving a
comment on a relevant issue that is already open.</p>
<p dir="auto">Our preferred channels of communication are all public, but if you’d like to
speak to us in private first, contact our community coordinators at
<a href="mailto:numpy-team@googlegroups.com">numpy-team@googlegroups.com</a> or on Slack (write <a href="mailto:numpy-team@googlegroups.com">numpy-team@googlegroups.com</a> for
an invitation).</p>
<p dir="auto">We also have a biweekly community call, details of which are announced on the
mailing list. You are very welcome to join.</p>
<p dir="auto">If you are new to contributing to open source, <a href="https://opensource.guide/how-to-contribute/" rel="nofollow">this
guide</a> helps explain why, what,
and how to successfully get involved.</p>
</article>
          </div>
